Hello Tom,
We still do not have the signed disclosures back or the response to the buyer's request. Without these
items and obtaining agreement on the request any talk of proceeds is premature. Because there simply
won't be any to divide.
We do not include escrow in any discussions on repair requests, so I have removed them from the email.
Mathieu still hasn't even opened the docusign for the request, let alone signed it. Please have these
documents signed immediately.
So that all parties know what to expect, it is very unlikely at this point that we close on Friday. If we got all
of these documents signed today, it is possible, but still very unlikely.
These buyers still have full cancellation rights. If they cancel because of the delays we go back on the
market with a very diminished appeal. If that happens a price reduction or relaunch with significant
investment are the only two options that would get the house sold. And either of those will take time to
find a buyer and hope they ask for less in concessions than these buyers have.
